# Elasticsearch Index Lifecycle Management Policy Engine

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in elastic/elasticsearch under x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/ and server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/ that implement Index Lifecycle Management (ILM). Identify: the IndexLifecycleService that triggers policy evaluation, the LifecyclePolicy and Phase model classes, the TransportPutLifecycleAction and TransportDeleteLifecycleAction handlers, the step execution framework (ClusterStateActionStep, AsyncWaitStep, AsyncActionStep), and the LifecycleExecutionState stored in index metadata. Report each file path and key class.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/elasticsearch--v8.17.0.

## ILM Implementation Files

### Core Service (`x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/`)
| Class | Role |
|-------|------|
| `IndexLifecycleService` | Triggers policy evaluation on cluster state changes and master elections |
| `IndexLifecycleRunner` | Dispatches step execution by type |
| `IndexLifecycleTransition` | Manages step/phase transitions |
| `ExecuteStepsUpdateTask` | Runs `ClusterStateActionStep`/`ClusterStateWaitStep` synchronously |
| `MoveToNextStepUpdateTask` | Advances index to next step in cluster state |
| `MoveToErrorStepUpdateTask` | Moves index to error step on failure |
| `PolicyStepsRegistry` | Caches compiled step lists per policy |
| `SetStepInfoUpdateTask` | Updates step info in index metadata |

### Transport/REST Actions (`action/` subpackage)
- **`TransportPutLifecycleAction`** and **`TransportDeleteLifecycleAction`** — CRUD for lifecycle policies
- Plus 9 other Transport handlers and 11 REST handlers

### Step Framework (`x-pack/plugin/core/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/core/ilm/`)
| Class | Role |
|-------|------|
| `LifecyclePolicy` | Top-level policy model with named phases |
| `Phase` | Phase model (hot/warm/cold/frozen/delete) with actions |
| `ClusterStateActionStep` | Abstract base for synchronous cluster state actions |
| `AsyncWaitStep` | Abstract base for async condition polling |
| `AsyncActionStep` | Abstract base for async transport actions |
| `ClusterStateWaitStep` | Abstract base for synchronous condition checks |

 \"text\": \"The Elasticsearch Index Lifecycle Management (ILM) implementation spans two main areas:\\n\\n**1. Service & Policy Evaluation (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/)**\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleService** (`IndexLifecycleService.java`): The central service that triggers policy evaluation. It listens to cluster state changes, checks if ILM is enabled, and invokes the `IndexLifecycleRunner` to run policy steps for each managed index. It is triggered both on master election (for async action steps) and on cluster state updates (for cluster state action/wait steps).\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleRunner** (`IndexLifecycleRunner.java`): Orchestrates the execution of individual lifecycle steps. It dispatches to the appropriate execution path depending on step type: `ClusterStateActionStep`, `ClusterStateWaitStep`, `AsyncActionStep`, or `AsyncWaitStep`.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleTransition** (`IndexLifecycleTransition.java`): Handles transitions between steps and phases in the lifecycle state machine.\\n\\n- **ExecuteStepsUpdateTask** (`ExecuteStepsUpdateTask.java`): A cluster state update task that runs `ClusterStateActionStep` and `ClusterStateWaitStep` steps synchronously within a cluster state update.\\n\\n- **MoveToNextStepUpdateTask** (`MoveToNextStepUpdateTask.java`): Updates the cluster state to advance an index to the next step.\\n\\n- **MoveToErrorStepUpdateTask** (`MoveToErrorStepUpdateTask.java`): Moves an index into the ILM error step when a step fails.\\n\\n- **SetStepInfoUpdateTask** (`SetStepInfoUpdateTask.java`): Updates step info in index metadata.\\n\\n- **PolicyStepsRegistry** (`PolicyStepsRegistry.java`): Maintains a registry of compiled step lists for each policy, keyed by policy name and version.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycle** (`IndexLifecycle.java`): The X-Pack plugin class registering ILM components.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask** (`IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask.java`): Base class for ILM cluster state update tasks.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleFeatures** (`IndexLifecycleFeatures.java`): Defines ILM feature metadata for the features API.\\n\\n- **IlmHealthIndicatorService** (`IlmHealthIndicatorService.java`): Health API integration for ILM.\\n\\n- **ReservedLifecycleStateHandlerProvider** (`ReservedLifecycleStateHandlerProvider.java`): Handles reserved state (file-based) ILM policy management.\\n\\n**2. Transport Action Handlers (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/action/)**\\n\\n- **TransportPutLifecycleAction** (`TransportPutLifecycleAction.java`): Handles PUT policy requests, storing `LifecyclePolicy` objects into cluster state via `IndexLifecycleMetadata`.\\n\\n- **TransportDeleteLifecycleAction** (`TransportDeleteLifecycleAction.java`): Handles DELETE policy requests.\\n\\n- **TransportGetLifecycleAction**, **TransportExplainLifecycleAction**, **TransportGetStatusAction**, **TransportMigrateToDataTiersAction**, **TransportMoveToStepAction**, **TransportRemoveIndexLifecyclePolicyAction**, **TransportRetryAction**, **TransportStartILMAction**, **TransportStopILMAction**: Additional transport action handlers for various ILM operations.\\n\\n- **ReservedLifecycleAction** (`ReservedLifecycleAction.java`): Reserved cluster state handler that applies ILM policies from configuration files.\\n\\n- REST handlers: `RestPutLifecycleAction`, `RestDeleteLifecycleAction`, `RestGetLifecycleAction`, `RestExplainLifecycleAction`, `RestGetStatusAction`, `RestMigrateToDataTiersAction`, `RestMoveToStepAction`, `RestRemoveIndexLifecyclePolicyAction`, `RestRetryAction`, `RestStartILMAction`, `RestStopAction`.\\n\\n**3. ILM History (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/history/)**\\n\\n- **ILMHistoryStore**, **ILMHistoryItem**, **ILMHistoryTemplateRegistry**: Record ILM step execution history to the `.ilm-history-*` index.\\n\\n**4. Cluster Metadata Helper (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/cluster/metadata/)**\\n\\n- **MetadataMigrateToDataTiersRoutingService** (`MetadataMigrateToDataTiersRoutingService.java`): Logic for migrating index/data stream allocation to data tiers.\\n\\n**5. Model Classes & Step Framework (x-pack/plugin/core/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/core/ilm/)**\\n\\n- **LifecyclePolicy** (`LifecyclePolicy.java`): Top-level model class representing a named ILM policy composed of named `Phase` objects.\\n\\n- **Phase** (`Phase.java`): Represents a lifecycle phase (hot, warm, cold, frozen, delete) with a minimum age and a set of `LifecycleAction` objects.\\n\\n- **Step** (`Step.java`): Base class for all lifecycle steps with a `StepKey` (phase/action/name triple).\\n\\n- **ClusterStateActionStep** (`ClusterStateActionStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that perform synchronous cluster state modifications (e.g., `InitializePolicyContextStep`, `GenerateUniqueIndexNameStep`, `CopySettingsStep`).\\n\\n- **ClusterStateWaitStep** (`ClusterStateWaitStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that check a condition synchronously against cluster state.\\n\\n- **AsyncActionStep** (`AsyncActionStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that perform asynchronous actions against the cluster (e.g., `ShrinkStep`, `RolloverStep`, `ForceMergeStep`, `DownsampleStep`).\\n\\n- **AsyncWaitStep** (`AsyncWaitStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that asynchronously poll a condition (e.g., `WaitForRolloverReadyStep`, `WaitForSnapshotStep`, `SegmentCountStep`).\\n\\n**6. LifecycleExecutionState (server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/)**\\n\\n- **LifecycleExecutionState** (`LifecycleExecutionState.java`): Stored in index metadata (custom metadata map), tracks the current lifecycle step (phase, action, step names), step start times, phase definition cache, and failure information for each ILM-managed index.\"\n}\n",

On master election it runs `AsyncActionStep` steps; on cluster state changes it runs `ClusterStateActionStep` and `ClusterStateWaitStep` steps, and schedules periodic polling for `AsyncWaitStep` steps.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleRunner** (`IndexLifecycleRunner.java`): Orchestrates execution of individual lifecycle steps, dispatching to the correct execution path based on step type.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleTransition** (`IndexLifecycleTransition.java`): Manages transitions between steps and phases.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycle** (`IndexLifecycle.java`): The X-Pack plugin registration class for all ILM components.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask** (`IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask.java`): Base class for cluster state update tasks used by ILM.\\n\\n- **ExecuteStepsUpdateTask** (`ExecuteStepsUpdateTask.java`): Cluster state update task that runs `ClusterStateActionStep` and `ClusterStateWaitStep` steps synchronously.\\n\\n- **MoveToNextStepUpdateTask** (`MoveToNextStepUpdateTask.java`): Updates cluster state to advance an index to the next step.\\n\\n- **MoveToErrorStepUpdateTask** (`MoveToErrorStepUpdateTask.java`): Moves an index into the ILM error step on failure.\\n\\n- **SetStepInfoUpdateTask** (`SetStepInfoUpdateTask.java`): Updates step info stored in index metadata.\\n\\n- **PolicyStepsRegistry** (`PolicyStepsRegistry.java`): Maintains a compiled cache of step lists per policy.\\n\\n- **IlmHealthIndicatorService** (`IlmHealthIndicatorService.java`): Health API integration for ILM status.\\n\\n- **ReservedLifecycleStateHandlerProvider** (`ReservedLifecycleStateHandlerProvider.java`): Handles file-based reserved cluster state ILM policies.\\n\\n**2. Transport & REST Action Handlers (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/action/)**\\n\\n- **TransportPutLifecycleAction**: Handles PUT policy requests, storing `LifecyclePolicy` into cluster state via `IndexLifecycleMetadata`.\\n- **TransportDeleteLifecycleAction**: Handles DELETE policy requests.\\n- **TransportGetLifecycleAction**, **TransportExplainLifecycleAction**, **TransportGetStatusAction**, **TransportMigrateToDataTiersAction**, **TransportMoveToStepAction**, **TransportRemoveIndexLifecyclePolicyAction**, **TransportRetryAction**, **TransportStartILMAction**, **TransportStopILMAction**: Additional transport handlers for ILM operations.\\n- **ReservedLifecycleAction**: Reserved state handler that uses `TransportPutLifecycleAction` and `TransportDeleteLifecycleAction` internally.\\n- REST handlers: `RestPutLifecycleAction`, `RestDeleteLifecycleAction`, `RestGetLifecycleAction`, `RestExplainLifecycleAction`, `RestGetStatusAction`, `RestMigrateToDataTiersAction`, `RestMoveToStepAction`, `RestRemoveIndexLifecyclePolicyAction`, `RestRetryAction`, `RestStartILMAction`, `RestStopAction`.\\n\\n**3. ILM History (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/history/)**\\n\\n- **ILMHistoryStore**, **ILMHistoryItem**, **ILMHistoryTemplateRegistry**: Record ILM step execution history to the `.ilm-history-*` index.\\n\\n**4. Cluster Metadata Helper (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/cluster/metadata/)**\\n\\n- **MetadataMigrateToDataTiersRoutingService**: Logic for migrating index/data stream allocation to data tiers.\\n\\n**5. Model Classes & Step Framework (x-pack/plugin/core/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/core/ilm/)**\\n\\n- **LifecyclePolicy** (`LifecyclePolicy.java`): Top-level model representing a named ILM policy composed of named `Phase` objects.\\n- **Phase** (`Phase.java`): Represents a lifecycle phase (hot, warm, cold, frozen, delete) with a minimum age and a set of `LifecycleAction` objects.\\n- **Step** (`Step.java`): Base class for all lifecycle steps, identified by a `StepKey` (phase/action/name triple).\\n- **ClusterStateActionStep** (`ClusterStateActionStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that perform synchronous cluster state modifications.\\n- **ClusterStateWaitStep** (`ClusterStateWaitStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that check a condition synchronously against cluster state.\\n- **AsyncActionStep** (`AsyncActionStep.java`): Abstract base for steps performing asynchronous transport actions (e.g., `ShrinkStep`, `RolloverStep`, `ForceMergeStep`).\\n- **AsyncWaitStep** (`AsyncWaitStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that periodically poll a condition asynchronously (e.g., `WaitForRolloverReadyStep`, `WaitForSnapshotStep`, `SegmentCountStep`).\\n\\n**6. LifecycleExecutionState (server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/)**\\n\\n- **LifecycleExecutionState** (`LifecycleExecutionState.java`): Stored in each index's custom metadata, tracking the current lifecycle step (phase, action, step names), step start times, phase definition cache, and failure details for each ILM-managed index.\"\n}\n",
  "file_path": "/workspace/answer.json"

\"ClusterStateWaitStep\"},\n    {\"repo\": \"sg-evals/elasticsearch--v8.17.0\", \"path\": \"x-pack/plugin/core/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/core/ilm/Step.java\", \"symbol\": \"Step\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Elasticsearch Index Lifecycle Management (ILM) implementation spans several modules:\\n\\n**1. Core Service & Policy Evaluation (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/)**\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleService** (`IndexLifecycleService.java`): The central service that triggers policy evaluation. It listens to cluster state changes and master elections, then invokes `IndexLifecycleRunner` to run policy steps for each managed index. On master election it runs `AsyncActionStep` steps; on cluster state changes it runs `ClusterStateActionStep` and `ClusterStateWaitStep` steps, and schedules periodic polling for `AsyncWaitStep` steps.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleRunner** (`IndexLifecycleRunner.java`): Orchestrates execution of individual lifecycle steps, dispatching to the correct execution path based on step type.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleTransition** (`IndexLifecycleTransition.java`): Manages transitions between steps and phases.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycle** (`IndexLifecycle.java`): The X-Pack plugin registration class for all ILM components.\\n\\n- **IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask** (`IndexLifecycleClusterStateUpdateTask.java`): Base class for cluster state update tasks used by ILM.\\n\\n- **ExecuteStepsUpdateTask** (`ExecuteStepsUpdateTask.java`): Cluster state update task that runs `ClusterStateActionStep` and `ClusterStateWaitStep` steps synchronously.\\n\\n- **MoveToNextStepUpdateTask** (`MoveToNextStepUpdateTask.java`): Updates cluster state to advance an index to the next step.\\n\\n- **MoveToErrorStepUpdateTask** (`MoveToErrorStepUpdateTask.java`): Moves an index into the ILM error step on failure.\\n\\n- **SetStepInfoUpdateTask** (`SetStepInfoUpdateTask.java`): Updates step info stored in index metadata.\\n\\n- **PolicyStepsRegistry** (`PolicyStepsRegistry.java`): Maintains a compiled cache of step lists per policy.\\n\\n- **IlmHealthIndicatorService** (`IlmHealthIndicatorService.java`): Health API integration for ILM status.\\n\\n- **ReservedLifecycleStateHandlerProvider** (`ReservedLifecycleStateHandlerProvider.java`): Handles file-based reserved cluster state ILM policies.\\n\\n**2. Transport & REST Action Handlers (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/action/)**\\n\\n- **TransportPutLifecycleAction**: Handles PUT policy requests, storing `LifecyclePolicy` into cluster state via `IndexLifecycleMetadata`.\\n- **TransportDeleteLifecycleAction**: Handles DELETE policy requests.\\n- **TransportGetLifecycleAction**, **TransportExplainLifecycleAction**, **TransportGetStatusAction**, **TransportMigrateToDataTiersAction**, **TransportMoveToStepAction**, **TransportRemoveIndexLifecyclePolicyAction**, **TransportRetryAction**, **TransportStartILMAction**, **TransportStopILMAction**: Additional transport handlers for ILM operations.\\n- **ReservedLifecycleAction**: Reserved state handler that uses `TransportPutLifecycleAction` and `TransportDeleteLifecycleAction` internally.\\n- REST handlers: `RestPutLifecycleAction`, `RestDeleteLifecycleAction`, `RestGetLifecycleAction`, `RestExplainLifecycleAction`, `RestGetStatusAction`, `RestMigrateToDataTiersAction`, `RestMoveToStepAction`, `RestRemoveIndexLifecyclePolicyAction`, `RestRetryAction`, `RestStartILMAction`, `RestStopAction`.\\n\\n**3. ILM History (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/ilm/history/)**\\n\\n- **ILMHistoryStore**, **ILMHistoryItem**, **ILMHistoryTemplateRegistry**: Record ILM step execution history to the `.ilm-history-*` index.\\n\\n**4. Cluster Metadata Helper (x-pack/plugin/ilm/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/cluster/metadata/)**\\n\\n- **MetadataMigrateToDataTiersRoutingService**: Logic for migrating index/data stream allocation to data tiers.\\n\\n**5. Model Classes & Step Framework (x-pack/plugin/core/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/xpack/core/ilm/)**\\n\\n- **LifecyclePolicy** (`LifecyclePolicy.java`): Top-level model representing a named ILM policy composed of named `Phase` objects.\\n- **Phase** (`Phase.java`): Represents a lifecycle phase (hot, warm, cold, frozen, delete) with a minimum age and a set of `LifecycleAction` objects.\\n- **Step** (`Step.java`): Base class for all lifecycle steps, identified by a `StepKey` (phase/action/name triple).\\n- **ClusterStateActionStep** (`ClusterStateActionStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that perform synchronous cluster state modifications.\\n- **ClusterStateWaitStep** (`ClusterStateWaitStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that check a condition synchronously against cluster state.\\n- **AsyncActionStep** (`AsyncActionStep.java`): Abstract base for steps performing asynchronous transport actions (e.g., `ShrinkStep`, `RolloverStep`, `ForceMergeStep`).\\n- **AsyncWaitStep** (`AsyncWaitStep.java`): Abstract base for steps that periodically poll a condition asynchronously (e.g., `WaitForRolloverReadyStep`, `WaitForSnapshotStep`, `SegmentCountStep`).\\n\\n**6. LifecycleExecutionState (server/src/main/java/org/elasticsearch/cluster/metadata/)**\\n\\n- **LifecycleExecutionState** (`LifecycleExecutionState.java`): Stored in each index's custom metadata, tracking the current lifecycle step (phase, action, step names), step start times, phase definition cache, and failure details for each ILM-managed index.\"\n}\n",
